------------------------ Physical Case Definition -----------------------
Compressible Euler equations.
Mach number: 1.
Angle of attack (AoA): 0 deg, and angle of sideslip (AoS): 0 deg.
No restart solution, use the values at infinity (freestream).
Dimensional simulation.
The reference area is 1 m^2.
The semi-span will be computed using the max y(3D) value.
The reference length is 1 m.
Surface(s) where the force coefficients are evaluated and
their reference origin for moment computation:
   - Nozzle (0.25, 0, 0).
   - Symmetry (0.25, 0, 0) m.
Surface(s) plotted in the output file: Symmetry.
Input mesh file name: Output_Mesh.su2

---------------------- Space Numerical Integration ----------------------
HLLC solver for the flow inviscid terms.
Second order integration in space, with slope limiter.
Venkatakrishnan slope-limiting method, with constant: 0.05.
The reference element size is: 1.
Gradient Computation using weighted Least-Squares method.

---------------------- Time Numerical Integration -----------------------
Local time stepping (steady state simulation).
Euler implicit method for the flow equations.
FGMRES is used for solving the linear system.
Using a LU-SGS preconditioning.
Convergence criteria of the linear solver: 1e-06.
Max number of linear iterations: 10.
W Multigrid Cycle, with 3 multigrid levels.
Damping factor for the residual restriction: 0.8.
Damping factor for the correction prolongation: 0.8.
CFL adaptation. Factor down: 1.5, factor up: 0.5,
                lower limit: 1, upper limit: 100.
Multigrid Level:                       0     1     2     3
Courant-Friedrichs-Lewy number:        4
MG PreSmooth coefficients:             1     2     3     3
MG PostSmooth coefficients:            0     0     0     0
MG CorrecSmooth coefficients:          0     0     0     0

------------------------- Convergence Criteria --------------------------
Maximum number of iterations: 10000.
Reduce the density residual 6 orders of magnitude.
The minimum bound for the density residual is 10^(-8).
Start convergence criteria at iteration 10.

-------------------------- Output Information ---------------------------
Writing a flow solution every 250 iterations.
Writing the convergence history every 1 iterations.
The output file format is Paraview ASCII (.vtk).
Convergence history file name: history.
Forces breakdown file name: forces_breakdown.dat.
Surface flow coefficients file name: surface_flow.
Flow variables file name: flow.
Restart flow file name: restart_flow.dat.

------------------- Config File Boundary Information --------------------
Euler wall boundary marker(s): Nozzle.
Far-field boundary marker(s): Inlet.
Symmetry plane boundary marker(s): Symmetry.
Supersonic outlet boundary marker(s): Outlet.

---------------------- Read Grid File Information -----------------------
Two dimensional problem.
13032 points.
4 surface markers.
60 boundary elements in index 0 (Marker = Outlet).
217 boundary elements in index 1 (Marker = Symmetry).
20 boundary elements in index 2 (Marker = Inlet).
233 boundary elements in index 3 (Marker = Nozzle).
25532 triangles.

------------------------- Geometry Preprocessing ------------------------
Setting point connectivity.
Renumbering points (Reverse Cuthill McKee Ordering).
Recomputing point connectivity.
Setting element connectivity.
Checking the numerical grid orientation.
There has been a re-orientation of the TRIANGLE volume elements.
There has been a re-orientation of the LINE surface elements.
Identifying edges and vertices.
Computing centers of gravity.
Setting the control volume structure.
Area of the computational grid: 25.9.
Searching for the closest normal neighbors to the surfaces.
Storing a mapping from global to local point index.
Compute the surface curvature.
Max K: 29.1. Mean K: 0.423. Standard deviation K: 3.32.
Checking for periodicity.
Setting the multigrid structure.
MG level: 0 -> CVs: 13032. Agglomeration rate 1/1.00. CFL 4.
MG level: 1 -> CVs: 3841. Agglomeration rate 1/3.39. CFL 3.26.
MG level: 2 -> CVs: 1100. Agglomeration rate 1/3.49. CFL 2.61.
MG level: 3 -> CVs: 322. Agglomeration rate 1/3.42. CFL 2.12.
Computing wall distances.
Wetted area = 11.1 m.
Area projection in the x-plane = 0 m, y-plane = 10.9 m.
Max. coordinate in the x-direction = 10.9 m, y-direction = 2.99 m.
Min coordinate in the x-direction = 0 m, y-direction = 1 m,.

------------------------- Driver information --------------------------
A Fluid driver has been instantiated.

------------------------ Iteration Preprocessing ------------------------
Zone 1: Euler/Navier-Stokes/RANS fluid iteration.

------------------------- Solver Preprocessing --------------------------
Inviscid flow: Computing density based on free-stream
temperature and pressure using the ideal gas law.
Force coefficients computed using free-stream values.

Fluid Model: STANDARD_AIR

Specific gas constant (non-dim): 287.058
Specific Heat Ratio: 1.4

------------------------ Physical Case Definition -----------------------
Compressible Euler equations.
Mach number: 1.
Angle of attack (AoA): 0 deg, and angle of sideslip (AoS): 0 deg.
No restart solution, use the values at infinity (freestream).
Dimensional simulation.
The reference area is 1 m^2.
The semi-span will be computed using the max y(3D) value.
The reference length is 1 m.
Surface(s) where the force coefficients are evaluated and
their reference origin for moment computation:
   - Nozzle (0.25, 0, 0).
   - Symmetry (0.25, 0, 0) m.
Surface(s) plotted in the output file: Symmetry.
Input mesh file name: Output_Mesh.su2

---------------------- Space Numerical Integration ----------------------
AUSM solver for the flow inviscid terms.
Second order integration in space, with slope limiter.
Venkatakrishnan slope-limiting method, with constant: 0.05.
The reference element size is: 1.
Gradient Computation using weighted Least-Squares method.

---------------------- Time Numerical Integration -----------------------
Local time stepping (steady state simulation).
Euler implicit method for the flow equations.
FGMRES is used for solving the linear system.
Using a LU-SGS preconditioning.
Convergence criteria of the linear solver: 1e-06.
Max number of linear iterations: 10.
W Multigrid Cycle, with 3 multigrid levels.
Damping factor for the residual restriction: 0.8.
Damping factor for the correction prolongation: 0.8.
No CFL adaptation.
Multigrid Level:                       0     1     2     3
Courant-Friedrichs-Lewy number:        4
MG PreSmooth coefficients:             1     2     3     3
MG PostSmooth coefficients:            0     0     0     0
MG CorrecSmooth coefficients:          0     0     0     0

------------------------- Convergence Criteria --------------------------
Maximum number of iterations: 10000.
Reduce the density residual 6 orders of magnitude.
The minimum bound for the density residual is 10^(-8).
Start convergence criteria at iteration 10.

-------------------------- Output Information ---------------------------
Writing a flow solution every 250 iterations.
Writing the convergence history every 1 iterations.
The output file format is Paraview ASCII (.vtk).
Convergence history file name: history.
Forces breakdown file name: forces_breakdown.dat.
Surface flow coefficients file name: surface_flow.
Flow variables file name: flow.
Restart flow file name: restart_flow.dat.

Far-field boundary marker(s): Inlet.
Symmetry plane boundary marker(s): Symmetry.
Supersonic outlet boundary marker(s): Outlet.

------------------------ Physical Case Definition -----------------------
Compressible Euler equations.
Mach number: 1.
Angle of attack (AoA): 0 deg, and angle of sideslip (AoS): 0 deg.
No restart solution, use the values at infinity (freestream).
Dimensional simulation.
The reference area is 1 m^2.
The semi-span will be computed using the max y(3D) value.
The reference length is 1 m.
Surface(s) where the force coefficients are evaluated and
their reference origin for moment computation:
   - Nozzle (0.25, 0, 0).
   - Symmetry (0.25, 0, 0) m.
Surface(s) plotted in the output file: Symmetry.
Input mesh file name: Output_Mesh.su2

---------------------- Space Numerical Integration ----------------------
HLLC solver for the flow inviscid terms.
First order integration in space.
Gradient Computation using weighted Least-Squares method.

---------------------- Time Numerical Integration -----------------------
Local time stepping (steady state simulation).
Euler implicit method for the flow equations.
FGMRES is used for solving the linear system.
Using a LU-SGS preconditioning.
Convergence criteria of the linear solver: 0.0001.
Max number of linear iterations: 10.
V Multigrid Cycle, with 2 multigrid levels.
Damping factor for the residual restriction: 0.8.
Damping factor for the correction prolongation: 0.8.
CFL adaptation. Factor down: 1.5, factor up: 0.5,
                lower limit: 1, upper limit: 100.
Multigrid Level:                       0     1     2
Courant-Friedrichs-Lewy number:        1
MG PreSmooth coefficients:             1     2     3
MG PostSmooth coefficients:            0     0     0
MG CorrecSmooth coefficients:          0     0     0

------------------------- Convergence Criteria --------------------------
Maximum number of iterations: 10000.
Reduce the density residual 6 orders of magnitude.
The minimum bound for the density residual is 10^(-8).
Start convergence criteria at iteration 10.

-------------------------- Output Information ---------------------------
Writing a flow solution every 250 iterations.
Writing the convergence history every 1 iterations.
The output file format is Paraview ASCII (.vtk).
Convergence history file name: history.
Forces breakdown file name: forces_breakdown.dat.
Surface flow coefficients file name: surface_flow.
Flow variables file name: flow.
Restart flow file name: restart_flow.dat.

------------------- Config File Boundary Information --------------------
Euler wall boundary marker(s): Nozzle.
Far-field boundary marker(s): Inlet.
Symmetry plane boundary marker(s): Symmetry.
Supersonic outlet boundary marker(s): Outlet.

---------------------- Read Grid File Information -----------------------
Two dimensional problem.
13032 points.
4 surface markers.
60 boundary elements in index 0 (Marker = Outlet).
217 boundary elements in index 1 (Marker = Symmetry).
20 boundary elements in index 2 (Marker = Inlet).
233 boundary elements in index 3 (Marker = Nozzle).
25532 triangles.

Setting point connectivity.

Checking the numerical grid orientation.

Identifying edges and vertices.
Computing centers of gravity.
Setting the control volume structure.

Storing a mapping from global to local point index.
Compute the surface curvature.

Checking for periodicity.
Setting the multigrid structure.
MG level: 0 -> CVs: 13032. Agglomeration rate 1/1.00. CFL 1.
MG level: 1 -> CVs: 3841. Agglomeration rate 1/3.39. CFL 0.814.
MG level: 2 -> CVs: 1100. Agglomeration rate 1/3.49. CFL 0.654.
Computing wall distances.

------------------------- Driver information --------------------------
A Fluid driver has been instantiated.

------------------------ Iteration Preprocessing ------------------------
Zone 1: Euler/Navier-Stokes/RANS fluid iteration.

------------------------- Solver Preprocessing --------------------------
Inviscid flow: Computing density based on free-stream
temperature and pressure using the ideal gas law.
Force coefficients computed using free-stream values.
